<pr_description>
The latest value, instead of the previous value,  is provided in $effect teardown if the state is a $derived
### Describe the bug

Not sure if this is a bug or intended. According to [this breaking change](https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/pull/15469), if the state caused an $effect to rerun, Svelte should provide the previous value of the state in the teardown function. This work for $state currently, but not for $derived, though it does work if $derived is reassigned. 

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/untitled?version=5.33.18#H4sIAAAAAAAACnWPy2rEMAxFf8WIgcl0woSuCm4SmC_oqqumizyU1tRVjKVkOgT_e3HS92MldHSPZM9A9TOChlsSIxY7SKE3Fhn03QxydnEWAaTvyaNzB57QSmRNzfgXbwcSJGHQkHPrjZOyokosimJVqA1LLZhc7q4_6II79GbCLuELXkZUyQb7HltJkp0qSjVHVEk7EA8WD3Z4SLaPRjFrtU0Vr5ZU4lFGT-qb9ENrzvjbC7GEXUV59vlsyptRZCA1UGtN-1TM617e70N57DrFebYmyv-z8X9XobyZ0J-8kXj7q-VK1mrmkGfurV36FUAKgi8CWvyI4T4FqY09GepA97VlDK_x94v_xwEAAA==

### Severity

annoyance
Incorrect prop value in onDestroy when there's a setter but not getter in the template
### Describe the bug

When a prop has a setter (for instance `<button onclick={() => (checked = !checked)}></button>`) but it doesn't have a getter (like `<p>{checked}</p>`), the value read during `onDestroy` does not match either the old or the current value of the prop, it's instead read as `null`.

This happens because the compiler decides to use `$.prop` to read the prop since it detects a "setter", `$.prop` "wraps" the prop in a `derived` but since we never read from it, when we execute `onDestroy` the `derived` is still in an "uninitialized" state hence it returns `null` instead of the correct value. 

### Reproduction

https://svelte.dev/playground/4fa745c18a3c41e88bda761f37b36783?version=5.34.9

Click `count++` twice, the 2nd time the `Component` is unmounted and `onDestroy` is called and it will log the incorrect `checked` value that should be `true` but is logged as `null`.

    49	export function validate_effect(rune) {

    51	                e.effect_orphan(rune);
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & UNOWNED) !== 0 && active_effect === null) {

    63	/**
    64	 * @param {Effect} effect
    65	 * @param {Effect} parent_effect
    66	 */
    67	function push_effect(effect, parent_effect) {
    68	        var parent_last = parent_effect.last;
    69	        if (parent_last === null) {
    70	                parent_effect.last = parent_effect.first = effect;
    71	        } else {
    72	                parent_last.next = effect;
    73	                effect.prev = parent_last;
    74	                parent_effect.last = effect;
    75	        }
    76	}

    78	/**
    79	 * @param {number} type
    80	 * @param {null | (() => void | (() => void))} fn
    81	 * @param {boolean} sync
    82	 * @param {boolean} push
    83	 * @returns {Effect}
    84	 */
    85	function create_effect(type, fn, sync, push = true) {
    86	        var parent = active_effect;
    87	
    88	        if (DEV) {
    89	                // Ensure the parent is never an inspect effect
    90	                while (parent !== null && (parent.f & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
    91	                        parent = parent.parent;
    92	                }
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        /** @type {Effect} */
    96	        var effect = {
    97	                ctx: component_context,
    98	                deps: null,
    99	                nodes_start: null,
   100	                nodes_end: null,
   101	                f: type | DIRTY,
   102	                first: null,
   103	                fn,
   104	                last: null,
   105	                next: null,
   106	                parent,
   107	                prev: null,
   108	                teardown: null,
   109	                transitions: null,
   110	                wv: 0,
   111	                ac: null
   112	        };
   113	
   114	        if (DEV) {
   115	                effect.component_function = dev_current_component_function;
   116	        }
   117	
   118	        if (sync) {
   119	                try {
   120	                        update_effect(effect);
   121	                        effect.f |= EFFECT_RAN;
   122	                } catch (e) {
   123	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   124	                        throw e;
   125	                }
   126	        } else if (fn !== null) {
   127	                schedule_effect(effect);
   128	        }
   129	
   130	        // if an effect has no dependencies, no DOM and no teardown function,
   131	        // don't bother adding it to the effect tree
   132	        var inert =
   133	                sync &&
   134	                effect.deps === null &&
   135	                effect.first === null &&
   136	                effect.nodes_start === null &&
   137	                effect.teardown === null &&
   138	                (effect.f & (EFFECT_HAS_DERIVED | BOUNDARY_EFFECT)) === 0;
   139	
   140	        if (!inert && push) {
   141	                if (parent !== null) {
   142	                        push_effect(effect, parent);
   143	                }
   144	
   145	                // if we're in a derived, add the effect there too
   146	                if (active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   147	                        var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (active_reaction);
   148	                        (derived.effects ??= []).push(effect);
   149	                }
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        return effect;
   153	}

   180	        // Non-nested `$effect(...)` in a component should be deferred
   181	        // until the component is mounted

   199	                        reaction: active_reaction

   240	/**
   241	 * An effect root whose children can transition out
   242	 * @param {() => void} fn
   243	 * @returns {(options?: { outro?: boolean }) => Promise<void>}
   244	 */
   245	export function component_root(fn) {
   246	        const effect = create_effect(ROOT_EFFECT, fn, true);
   247	
   248	        return (options = {}) => {
   249	                return new Promise((fulfil) => {
   250	                        if (options.outro) {
   251	                                pause_effect(effect, () => {
   252	                                        destroy_effect(effect);
   253	                                        fulfil(undefined);
   254	                                });
   255	                        } else {
   256	                                destroy_effect(effect);
   257	                                fulfil(undefined);
   258	                        }
   259	                });
   260	        };
   261	}

   271	/**
   272	 * Internal representation of `$: ..`
   273	 * @param {() => any} deps
   274	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   275	 */
   276	export function legacy_pre_effect(deps, fn) {
   277	        var context = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (component_context);
   278	
   279	        /** @type {{ effect: null | Effect, ran: boolean }} */
   280	        var token = { effect: null, ran: false };
   281	        context.l.r1.push(token);
   282	
   283	        token.effect = render_effect(() => {
   284	                deps();
   285	
   286	                // If this legacy pre effect has already run before the end of the reset, then
   287	                // bail out to emulate the same behavior.
   288	                if (token.ran) return;
   289	
   290	                token.ran = true;
   291	                set(context.l.r2, true);
   292	                untrack(fn);
   293	        });
   294	}
   295	
   296	export function legacy_pre_effect_reset() {
   297	        var context = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (component_context);
   298	
   299	        render_effect(() => {
   300	                if (!get(context.l.r2)) return;
   301	
   302	                // Run dirty `$:` statements
   303	                for (var token of context.l.r1) {
   304	                        var effect = token.effect;
   305	
   306	                        // If the effect is CLEAN, then make it MAYBE_DIRTY. This ensures we traverse through
   307	                        // the effects dependencies and correctly ensure each dependency is up-to-date.
   308	                        if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   309	                                set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   310	                        }
   311	
   312	                        if (check_dirtiness(effect)) {
   313	                                update_effect(effect);
   314	                        }
   315	
   316	                        token.ran = false;
   317	                }
   318	
   319	                context.l.r2.v = false; // set directly to avoid rerunning this effect
   320	        });
   321	}

   323	/**
   324	 * @param {() => void | (() => void)} fn
   325	 * @returns {Effect}

   327	export function render_effect(fn) {
   328	        return create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT, fn, true);
   329	}
   330	
   331	/**
   332	 * @param {(...expressions: any) => void | (() => void)} fn
   333	 * @param {Array<() => any>} thunks
   334	 * @param {<T>(fn: () => T) => Derived<T>} d
   335	 * @returns {Effect}
   336	 */
   337	export function template_effect(fn, thunks = [], d = derived) {
   338	        if (DEV) {
   339	                // wrap the effect so that we can decorate stack trace with `in {expression}`
   340	                // (TODO maybe there's a better approach?)
   341	                return render_effect(() => {
   342	                        var outer = /** @type {Effect} */ (active_effect);
   343	                        var inner = () => fn(...deriveds.map(get));
   344	
   345	                        define_property(outer.fn, 'name', { value: '{expression}' });
   346	                        define_property(inner, 'name', { value: '{expression}' });
   347	
   348	                        const deriveds = thunks.map(d);
   349	                        block(inner);
   350	                });
   351	        }
   352	
   353	        const deriveds = thunks.map(d);
   354	        return block(() => fn(...deriveds.map(get)));
   355	}
   356	
   357	/**
   358	 * @param {(() => void)} fn
   359	 * @param {number} flags
   360	 */
   361	export function block(fn, flags = 0) {
   362	        var effect = create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT | BLOCK_EFFECT | flags, fn, true);
   363	        if (DEV) {
   364	                effect.dev_stack = dev_stack;
   365	        }
   366	        return effect;
   367	}

   369	/**
   370	 * @param {(() => void)} fn
   371	 * @param {boolean} [push]
   372	 */
   373	export function branch(fn, push = true) {
   374	        return create_effect(RENDER_EFFECT | BRANCH_EFFECT, fn, true, push);
   375	}
   376	
   377	/**
   378	 * @param {Effect} effect
   379	 */
   380	export function execute_effect_teardown(effect) {
   381	        var teardown = effect.teardown;
   382	        if (teardown !== null) {
   383	                const previously_destroying_effect = is_destroying_effect;
   384	                const previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   385	                set_is_destroying_effect(true);
   386	                set_active_reaction(null);
   387	                try {
   388	                        teardown.call(null);
   389	                } finally {
   390	                        set_is_destroying_effect(previously_destroying_effect);
   391	                        set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   392	                }
   393	        }
   394	}
   395	
   396	/**
   397	 * @param {Effect} signal
   398	 * @param {boolean} remove_dom
   399	 * @returns {void}
   400	 */
   401	export function destroy_effect_children(signal, remove_dom = false) {
   402	        var effect = signal.first;
   403	        signal.first = signal.last = null;
   404	
   405	        while (effect !== null) {
   406	                effect.ac?.abort(STALE_REACTION);
   407	
   408	                var next = effect.next;
   409	
   410	                if ((effect.f & ROOT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   411	                        // this is now an independent root
   412	                        effect.parent = null;
   413	                } else {
   414	                        destroy_effect(effect, remove_dom);
   415	                }
   416	
   417	                effect = next;
   418	        }
   419	}
   420	
   421	/**
   422	 * @param {Effect} signal
   423	 * @returns {void}
   424	 */
   425	export function destroy_block_effect_children(signal) {
   426	        var effect = signal.first;
   427	
   428	        while (effect !== null) {
   429	                var next = effect.next;
   430	                if ((effect.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) === 0) {
   431	                        destroy_effect(effect);
   432	                }
   433	                effect = next;
   434	        }
   435	}
   436	
   437	/**
   438	 * @param {Effect} effect
   439	 * @param {boolean} [remove_dom]
   440	 * @returns {void}
   441	 */
   442	export function destroy_effect(effect, remove_dom = true) {
   443	        var removed = false;
   444	
   445	        if (
   446	                (remove_dom || (effect.f & HEAD_EFFECT) !== 0) &&
   447	                effect.nodes_start !== null &&
   448	                effect.nodes_end !== null
   449	        ) {
   450	                remove_effect_dom(effect.nodes_start, /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (effect.nodes_end));
   451	                removed = true;
   452	        }
   453	
   454	        destroy_effect_children(effect, remove_dom && !removed);
   455	        remove_reactions(effect, 0);
   456	        set_signal_status(effect, DESTROYED);
   457	
   458	        var transitions = effect.transitions;
   459	
   460	        if (transitions !== null) {
   461	                for (const transition of transitions) {
   462	                        transition.stop();
   463	                }
   464	        }
   465	
   466	        execute_effect_teardown(effect);
   467	
   468	        var parent = effect.parent;
   469	
   470	        // If the parent doesn't have any children, then skip this work altogether
   471	        if (parent !== null && parent.first !== null) {
   472	                unlink_effect(effect);
   473	        }
   474	
   475	        if (DEV) {
   476	                effect.component_function = null;
   477	        }
   478	
   479	        // `first` and `child` are nulled out in destroy_effect_children
   480	        // we don't null out `parent` so that error propagation can work correctly
   481	        effect.next =
   482	                effect.prev =
   483	                effect.teardown =
   484	                effect.ctx =
   485	                effect.deps =
   486	                effect.fn =
   487	                effect.nodes_start =
   488	                effect.nodes_end =
   489	                effect.ac =
   490	                        null;
   491	}
   492	
   493	/**
   494	 *
   495	 * @param {TemplateNode | null} node
   496	 * @param {TemplateNode} end
   497	 */
   498	export function remove_effect_dom(node, end) {
   499	        while (node !== null) {
   500	                /** @type {TemplateNode | null} */
   501	                var next = node === end ? null : /** @type {TemplateNode} */ (get_next_sibling(node));
   502	
   503	                node.remove();
   504	                node = next;
   505	        }
   506	}
   507	
   508	/**
   509	 * Detach an effect from the effect tree, freeing up memory and
   510	 * reducing the amount of work that happens on subsequent traversals
   511	 * @param {Effect} effect
   512	 */
   513	export function unlink_effect(effect) {
   514	        var parent = effect.parent;
   515	        var prev = effect.prev;
   516	        var next = effect.next;
   517	
   518	        if (prev !== null) prev.next = next;
   519	        if (next !== null) next.prev = prev;
   520	
   521	        if (parent !== null) {
   522	                if (parent.first === effect) parent.first = next;
   523	                if (parent.last === effect) parent.last = prev;
   524	        }
   525	}
   526	
   527	/**
   528	 * When a block effect is removed, we don't immediately destroy it or yank it
   529	 * out of the DOM, because it might have transitions. Instead, we 'pause' it.
   530	 * It stays around (in memory, and in the DOM) until outro transitions have
   531	 * completed, and if the state change is reversed then we _resume_ it.
   532	 * A paused effect does not update, and the DOM subtree becomes inert.
   533	 * @param {Effect} effect
   534	 * @param {() => void} [callback]
   535	 */
   536	export function pause_effect(effect, callback) {
   537	        /** @type {TransitionManager[]} */
   538	        var transitions = [];
   539	
   540	        pause_children(effect, transitions, true);
   541	
   542	        run_out_transitions(transitions, () => {
   543	                destroy_effect(effect);
   544	                if (callback) callback();
   545	        });
   546	}
   547	
   548	/**
   549	 * @param {TransitionManager[]} transitions
   550	 * @param {() => void} fn
   551	 */
   552	export function run_out_transitions(transitions, fn) {
   553	        var remaining = transitions.length;
   554	        if (remaining > 0) {
   555	                var check = () => --remaining || fn();
   556	                for (var transition of transitions) {
   557	                        transition.out(check);
   558	                }
   559	        } else {
   560	                fn();
   561	        }
   562	}
   563	
   564	/**
   565	 * @param {Effect} effect
   566	 * @param {TransitionManager[]} transitions
   567	 * @param {boolean} local
   568	 */
   569	export function pause_children(effect, transitions, local) {
   570	        if ((effect.f & INERT) !== 0) return;
   571	        effect.f ^= INERT;
   572	
   573	        if (effect.transitions !== null) {
   574	                for (const transition of effect.transitions) {
   575	                        if (transition.is_global || local) {
   576	                                transitions.push(transition);
   577	                        }
   578	                }
   579	        }
   580	
   581	        var child = effect.first;
   582	
   583	        while (child !== null) {
   584	                var sibling = child.next;
   585	                var transparent = (child.f & EFFECT_TRANSPARENT) !== 0 || (child.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0;
   586	                // TODO we don't need to call pause_children recursively with a linked list in place
   587	                // it's slightly more involved though as we have to account for `transparent` changing
   588	                // through the tree.
   589	                pause_children(child, transitions, transparent ? local : false);
   590	                child = sibling;
   591	        }
   592	}
   593	
   594	/**
   595	 * The opposite of `pause_effect`. We call this if (for example)
   596	 * `x` becomes falsy then truthy: `{#if x}...{/if}`
   597	 * @param {Effect} effect
   598	 */
   599	export function resume_effect(effect) {
   600	        resume_children(effect, true);
   601	}
   602	
   603	/**
   604	 * @param {Effect} effect
   605	 * @param {boolean} local
   606	 */
   607	function resume_children(effect, local) {
   608	        if ((effect.f & INERT) === 0) return;
   609	        effect.f ^= INERT;
   610	
   611	        var child = effect.first;
   612	
   613	        while (child !== null) {
   614	                var sibling = child.next;
   615	                var transparent = (child.f & EFFECT_TRANSPARENT) !== 0 || (child.f & BRANCH_EFFECT) !== 0;
   616	                // TODO we don't need to call resume_children recursively with a linked list in place
   617	                // it's slightly more involved though as we have to account for `transparent` changing
   618	                // through the tree.
   619	                resume_children(child, transparent ? local : false);
   620	                child = sibling;
   621	        }
   622	
   623	        if (effect.transitions !== null) {
   624	                for (const transition of effect.transitions) {
   625	                        if (transition.is_global || local) {
   626	                                transition.in();
   627	                        }
   628	                }
   629	        }
   630	}
   631

   151	/**
   152	 * Determines whether a derived or effect is dirty.
   153	 * If it is MAYBE_DIRTY, will set the status to CLEAN
   154	 * @param {Reaction} reaction
   155	 * @returns {boolean}
   156	 */
   157	export function check_dirtiness(reaction) {
   158	        var flags = reaction.f;
   159	
   160	        if ((flags & DIRTY) !== 0) {
   161	                return true;
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        if ((flags & MAYBE_DIRTY) !== 0) {
   165	                var dependencies = reaction.deps;
   166	                var is_unowned = (flags & UNOWNED) !== 0;
   167	
   168	                if (dependencies !== null) {
   169	                        var i;
   170	                        var dependency;
   171	                        var is_disconnected = (flags & DISCONNECTED) !== 0;
   172	                        var is_unowned_connected = is_unowned && active_effect !== null && !skip_reaction;
   173	                        var length = dependencies.length;
   174	
   175	                        // If we are working with a disconnected or an unowned signal that is now connected (due to an active effect)
   176	                        // then we need to re-connect the reaction to the dependency
   177	                        if (is_disconnected || is_unowned_connected) {
   178	                                var derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (reaction);
   179	                                var parent = derived.parent;
   180	
   181	                                for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   182	                                        dependency = dependencies[i];
   183	
   184	                                        // We always re-add all reactions (even duplicates) if the derived was
   185	                                        // previously disconnected, however we don't if it was unowned as we
   186	                                        // de-duplicate dependencies in that case
   187	                                        if (is_disconnected || !dependency?.reactions?.includes(derived)) {
   188	                                                (dependency.reactions ??= []).push(derived);
   189	                                        }
   190	                                }
   191	
   192	                                if (is_disconnected) {
   193	                                        derived.f ^= DISCONNECTED;
   194	                                }
   195	                                // If the unowned derived is now fully connected to the graph again (it's unowned and reconnected, has a parent
   196	                                // and the parent is not unowned), then we can mark it as connected again, removing the need for the unowned
   197	                                // flag
   198	                                if (is_unowned_connected && parent !== null && (parent.f & UNOWNED) === 0) {
   199	                                        derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
   200	                                }
   201	                        }
   202	
   203	                        for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   204	                                dependency = dependencies[i];
   205	
   206	                                if (check_dirtiness(/** @type {Derived} */ (dependency))) {
   207	                                        update_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (dependency));
   208	                                }
   209	
   210	                                if (dependency.wv > reaction.wv) {
   211	                                        return true;
   212	                                }
   213	                        }
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                // Unowned signals should never be marked as clean unless they
   217	                // are used within an active_effect without skip_reaction
   218	                if (!is_unowned || (active_effect !== null && !skip_reaction)) {
   219	                        set_signal_status(reaction, CLEAN);
   220	                }
   221	        }
   222	
   223	        return false;
   224	}
   225	
   226	/**
   227	 * @param {Value} signal
   228	 * @param {Effect} effect
   229	 * @param {boolean} [root]
   230	 */
   231	function schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(signal, effect, root = true) {
   232	        var reactions = signal.reactions;
   233	        if (reactions === null) return;
   234	
   235	        for (var i = 0; i < reactions.length; i++) {
   236	                var reaction = reactions[i];
   237	
   238	                if (reaction_sources?.[1].includes(signal) && reaction_sources[0] === active_reaction) continue;
   239	
   240	                if ((reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   241	                        schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(/** @type {Derived} */ (reaction), effect, false);
   242	                } else if (effect === reaction) {
   243	                        if (root) {
   244	                                set_signal_status(reaction, DIRTY);
   245	                        } else if ((reaction.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   246	                                set_signal_status(reaction, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   247	                        }
   248	                        schedule_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (reaction));
   249	                }
   250	        }
   251	}
   252	
   253	/** @param {Reaction} reaction */
   254	export function update_reaction(reaction) {
   255	        var previous_deps = new_deps;
   256	        var previous_skipped_deps = skipped_deps;
   257	        var previous_untracked_writes = untracked_writes;
   258	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   259	        var previous_skip_reaction = skip_reaction;
   260	        var previous_reaction_sources = reaction_sources;
   261	        var previous_component_context = component_context;
   262	        var previous_untracking = untracking;
   263	
   264	        var flags = reaction.f;
   265	
   266	        new_deps = /** @type {null | Value[]} */ (null);
   267	        skipped_deps = 0;
   268	        untracked_writes = null;
   269	        skip_reaction =
   270	                (flags & UNOWNED) !== 0 && (untracking || !is_updating_effect || active_reaction === null);
   271	        active_reaction = (flags & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0 ? reaction : null;
   272	
   273	        reaction_sources = null;
   274	        set_component_context(reaction.ctx);
   275	        untracking = false;
   276	        read_version++;
   277	
   278	        reaction.f |= EFFECT_IS_UPDATING;
   279	
   280	        if (reaction.ac !== null) {
   281	                reaction.ac.abort(STALE_REACTION);
   282	                reaction.ac = null;
   283	        }
   284	
   285	        try {
   286	                var result = /** @type {Function} */ (0, reaction.fn)();
   287	                var deps = reaction.deps;
   288	
   289	                if (new_deps !== null) {
   290	                        var i;
   291	
   292	                        remove_reactions(reaction, skipped_deps);
   293	
   294	                        if (deps !== null && skipped_deps > 0) {
   295	                                deps.length = skipped_deps + new_deps.length;
   296	                                for (i = 0; i < new_deps.length; i++) {
   297	                                        deps[skipped_deps + i] = new_deps[i];
   298	                                }
   299	                        } else {
   300	                                reaction.deps = deps = new_deps;
   301	                        }
   302	
   303	                        if (
   304	                                !skip_reaction ||
   305	                                // Deriveds that already have reactions can cleanup, so we still add them as reactions
   306	                                ((flags & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   307	                                        /** @type {import('#client').Derived} */ (reaction).reactions !== null)
   308	                        ) {
   309	                                for (i = skipped_deps; i < deps.length; i++) {
   310	                                        (deps[i].reactions ??= []).push(reaction);
   311	                                }
   312	                        }
   313	                } else if (deps !== null && skipped_deps < deps.length) {
   314	                        remove_reactions(reaction, skipped_deps);
   315	                        deps.length = skipped_deps;
   316	                }
   317	
   318	                // If we're inside an effect and we have untracked writes, then we need to
   319	                // ensure that if any of those untracked writes result in re-invalidation
   320	                // of the current effect, then that happens accordingly
   321	                if (
   322	                        is_runes() &&
   323	                        untracked_writes !== null &&
   324	                        !untracking &&
   325	                        deps !== null &&
   326	                        (reaction.f & (DERIVED | MAYBE_DIRTY | DIRTY)) === 0
   327	                ) {
   328	                        for (i = 0; i < /** @type {Source[]} */ (untracked_writes).length; i++) {
   329	                                schedule_possible_effect_self_invalidation(
   330	                                        untracked_writes[i],
   331	                                        /** @type {Effect} */ (reaction)
   332	                                );
   333	                        }
   334	                }
   335	
   336	                // If we are returning to an previous reaction then
   337	                // we need to increment the read version to ensure that
   338	                // any dependencies in this reaction aren't marked with
   339	                // the same version
   340	                if (previous_reaction !== null && previous_reaction !== reaction) {
   341	                        read_version++;
   342	
   343	                        if (untracked_writes !== null) {
   344	                                if (previous_untracked_writes === null) {
   345	                                        previous_untracked_writes = untracked_writes;
   346	                                } else {
   347	                                        previous_untracked_writes.push(.../** @type {Source[]} */ (untracked_writes));
   348	                                }
   349	                        }
   350	                }
   351	
   352	                return result;
   353	        } catch (error) {
   354	                handle_error(error);
   355	        } finally {
   356	                new_deps = previous_deps;
   357	                skipped_deps = previous_skipped_deps;
   358	                untracked_writes = previous_untracked_writes;
   359	                active_reaction = previous_reaction;
   360	                skip_reaction = previous_skip_reaction;
   361	                reaction_sources = previous_reaction_sources;
   362	                set_component_context(previous_component_context);
   363	                untracking = previous_untracking;
   364	
   365	                reaction.f ^= EFFECT_IS_UPDATING;
   366	        }
   367	}
   368	
   369	/**
   370	 * @template V
   371	 * @param {Reaction} signal
   372	 * @param {Value<V>} dependency
   373	 * @returns {void}
   374	 */
   375	function remove_reaction(signal, dependency) {
   376	        let reactions = dependency.reactions;
   377	        if (reactions !== null) {
   378	                var index = index_of.call(reactions, signal);
   379	                if (index !== -1) {
   380	                        var new_length = reactions.length - 1;
   381	                        if (new_length === 0) {
   382	                                reactions = dependency.reactions = null;
   383	                        } else {
   384	                                // Swap with last element and then remove.
   385	                                reactions[index] = reactions[new_length];
   386	                                reactions.pop();
   387	                        }
   388	                }
   389	        }
   390	        // If the derived has no reactions, then we can disconnect it from the graph,
   391	        // allowing it to either reconnect in the future, or be GC'd by the VM.
   392	        if (
   393	                reactions === null &&
   394	                (dependency.f & DERIVED) !== 0 &&
   395	                // Destroying a child effect while updating a parent effect can cause a dependency to appear
   396	                // to be unused, when in fact it is used by the currently-updating parent. Checking `new_deps`
   397	                // allows us to skip the expensive work of disconnecting and immediately reconnecting it
   398	                (new_deps === null || !new_deps.includes(dependency))
   399	        ) {
   400	                set_signal_status(dependency, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   401	                // If we are working with a derived that is owned by an effect, then mark it as being
   402	                // disconnected.
   403	                if ((dependency.f & (UNOWNED | DISCONNECTED)) === 0) {
   404	                        dependency.f ^= DISCONNECTED;
   405	                }
   406	                // Disconnect any reactions owned by this reaction
   407	                destroy_derived_effects(/** @type {Derived} **/ (dependency));
   408	                remove_reactions(/** @type {Derived} **/ (dependency), 0);
   409	        }
   410	}
   411	
   412	/**
   413	 * @param {Reaction} signal
   414	 * @param {number} start_index
   415	 * @returns {void}
   416	 */
   417	export function remove_reactions(signal, start_index) {
   418	        var dependencies = signal.deps;
   419	        if (dependencies === null) return;
   420	
   421	        for (var i = start_index; i < dependencies.length; i++) {
   422	                remove_reaction(signal, dependencies[i]);
   423	        }
   424	}
   425	
   426	/**
   427	 * @param {Effect} effect
   428	 * @returns {void}
   429	 */
   430	export function update_effect(effect) {
   431	        var flags = effect.f;
   432	
   433	        if ((flags & DESTROYED) !== 0) {
   434	                return;
   435	        }
   436	
   437	        set_signal_status(effect, CLEAN);
   438	
   439	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   440	        var was_updating_effect = is_updating_effect;
   441	
   442	        active_effect = effect;
   443	        is_updating_effect = true;
   444	
   445	        if (DEV) {
   446	                var previous_component_fn = dev_current_component_function;
   447	                set_dev_current_component_function(effect.component_function);
   448	                var previous_stack = /** @type {any} */ (dev_stack);
   449	                // only block effects have a dev stack, keep the current one otherwise
   450	                set_dev_stack(effect.dev_stack ?? dev_stack);
   451	        }
   452	
   453	        try {
   454	                if ((flags & BLOCK_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   455	                        destroy_block_effect_children(effect);
   456	                } else {
   457	                        destroy_effect_children(effect);
   458	                }
   459	
   460	                execute_effect_teardown(effect);
   461	                var teardown = update_reaction(effect);
   462	                effect.teardown = typeof teardown === 'function' ? teardown : null;
   463	                effect.wv = write_version;
   464	
   465	                // In DEV, increment versions of any sources that were written to during the effect,
   466	                // so that they are correctly marked as dirty when the effect re-runs
   467	                if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag && (effect.f & DIRTY) !== 0 && effect.deps !== null) {
   468	                        for (var dep of effect.deps) {
   469	                                if (dep.set_during_effect) {
   470	                                        dep.wv = increment_write_version();
   471	                                        dep.set_during_effect = false;
   472	                                }
   473	                        }
   474	                }
   475	
   476	                if (DEV) {
   477	                        dev_effect_stack.push(effect);
   478	                }
   479	        } finally {
   480	                is_updating_effect = was_updating_effect;
   481	                active_effect = previous_effect;
   482	
   483	                if (DEV) {
   484	                        set_dev_current_component_function(previous_component_fn);
   485	                        set_dev_stack(previous_stack);
   486	                }
   487	        }
   488	}
   489	
   490	function log_effect_stack() {
   491	        // eslint-disable-next-line no-console
   492	        console.error(
   493	                'Last ten effects were: ',
   494	                dev_effect_stack.slice(-10).map((d) => d.fn)
   495	        );
   496	        dev_effect_stack = [];
   497	}
   498	
   499	function infinite_loop_guard() {
   500	        try {
   501	                e.effect_update_depth_exceeded();
   502	        } catch (error) {
   503	                if (DEV) {
   504	                        // stack is garbage, ignore. Instead add a console.error message.
   505	                        define_property(error, 'stack', {
   506	                                value: ''
   507	                        });
   508	                }
   509	                // Try and handle the error so it can be caught at a boundary, that's
   510	                // if there's an effect available from when it was last scheduled
   511	                if (last_scheduled_effect !== null) {
   512	                        if (DEV) {
   513	                                try {
   514	                                        invoke_error_boundary(error, last_scheduled_effect);
   515	                                } catch (e) {
   516	                                        // Only log the effect stack if the error is re-thrown
   517	                                        log_effect_stack();
   518	                                        throw e;
   519	                                }
   520	                        } else {
   521	                                invoke_error_boundary(error, last_scheduled_effect);
   522	                        }
   523	                } else {
   524	                        if (DEV) {
   525	                                log_effect_stack();
   526	                        }
   527	                        throw error;
   528	                }
   529	        }
   530	}
   531	
   532	function flush_queued_root_effects() {
   533	        var was_updating_effect = is_updating_effect;
   534	
   535	        try {
   536	                var flush_count = 0;
   537	                is_updating_effect = true;
   538	
   539	                while (queued_root_effects.length > 0) {
   540	                        if (flush_count++ > 1000) {
   541	                                infinite_loop_guard();
   542	                        }
   543	
   544	                        var root_effects = queued_root_effects;
   545	                        var length = root_effects.length;
   546	
   547	                        queued_root_effects = [];
   548	
   549	                        for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   550	                                var collected_effects = process_effects(root_effects[i]);
   551	                                flush_queued_effects(collected_effects);
   552	                        }
   553	                        old_values.clear();
   554	                }
   555	        } finally {
   556	                is_flushing = false;
   557	                is_updating_effect = was_updating_effect;
   558	
   559	                last_scheduled_effect = null;
   560	                if (DEV) {
   561	                        dev_effect_stack = [];
   562	                }
   563	        }
   564	}
   565	
   566	/**
   567	 * @param {Array<Effect>} effects
   568	 * @returns {void}
   569	 */
   570	function flush_queued_effects(effects) {
   571	        var length = effects.length;

   136	        if (
   137	                active_reaction !== null &&

   139	                // to ensure we error if state is set inside an inspect effect

   164	        if (!source.equals(value)) {
   165	                var old_value = source.v;
   166	
   167	                if (is_destroying_effect) {
   168	                        old_values.set(source, value);
   169	                } else {
   170	                        old_values.set(source, old_value);
   171	                }
   172	
   173	                source.v = value;
   174	
   175	                if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag) {
   176	                        source.updated = get_stack('UpdatedAt');
   177	
   178	                        if (active_effect !== null) {
   179	                                source.set_during_effect = true;
   180	                        }
   181	                }
   182	
   183	                if ((source.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   184	                        // if we are assigning to a dirty derived we set it to clean/maybe dirty but we also eagerly execute it to track the dependencies
   185	                        if ((source.f & DIRTY) !== 0) {
   186	                                execute_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (source));
   187	                        }
   188	                        set_signal_status(source, (source.f & UNOWNED) === 0 ? CLEAN : MAYBE_DIRTY);
   189	                }
   190	
   191	                source.wv = increment_write_version();
   192	
   193	                mark_reactions(source, DIRTY);
   194	
   195	                // It's possible that the current reaction might not have up-to-date dependencies
   196	                // whilst it's actively running. So in the case of ensuring it registers the reaction
   197	                // properly for itself, we need to ensure the current effect actually gets
   198	                // scheduled. i.e: `$effect(() => x++)`
   199	                if (
   200	                        is_runes() &&
   201	                        active_effect !== null &&
   202	                        (active_effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0 &&
   203	                        (active_effect.f & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0
   204	                ) {
   205	                        if (untracked_writes === null) {
   206	                                set_untracked_writes([source]);
   207	                        } else {
   208	                                untracked_writes.push(source);
   209	                        }
   210	                }
   211	
   212	                if (DEV && inspect_effects.size > 0) {
   213	                        const inspects = Array.from(inspect_effects);
   214	
   215	                        for (const effect of inspects) {
   216	                                // Mark clean inspect-effects as maybe dirty and then check their dirtiness
   217	                                // instead of just updating the effects - this way we avoid overfiring.
   218	                                if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   219	                                        set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   220	                                }
   221	                                if (check_dirtiness(effect)) {
   222	                                        update_effect(effect);
   223	                                }
   224	                        }
   225	
   226	                        inspect_effects.clear();
   227	                }
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        return value;
   231	}
   232	
   233	/**
   234	 * @template {number | bigint} T
   235	 * @param {Source<T>} source
   236	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
   237	 * @returns {T}
   238	 */
   239	export function update(source, d = 1) {
   240	        var value = get(source);
   241	        var result = d === 1 ? value++ : value--;
   242	
   243	        set(source, value);
   244	
   245	        // @ts-expect-error
   246	        return result;
   247	}
   248

   251	 * @param {Source<T>} source

   255	export function update_pre(source, d = 1) {
   256	        var value = get(source);
   257	
   258	        // @ts-expect-error
   259	        return set(source, d === 1 ? ++value : --value);
   260	}

   262	/**
   263	 * @param {Value} signal
   264	 * @param {number} status should be DIRTY or MAYBE_DIRTY
   265	 * @returns {void}
   266	 */
   267	function mark_reactions(signal, status) {
   268	        var reactions = signal.reactions;
   269	        if (reactions === null) return;
   270	
   271	        var runes = is_runes();
   272	        var length = reactions.length;
   273	
   274	        for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   275	                var reaction = reactions[i];
   276	                var flags = reaction.f;
   277	
   278	                // Skip any effects that are already dirty
   279	                if ((flags & DIRTY) !== 0) continue;
   280	
   281	                // In legacy mode, skip the current effect to prevent infinite loops
   282	                if (!runes && reaction === active_effect) continue;
   283	
   284	                // Inspect effects need to run immediately, so that the stack trace makes sense
   285	                if (DEV && (flags & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   286	                        inspect_effects.add(reaction);
   287	                        continue;
   288	                }
   289	
   290	                set_signal_status(reaction, status);
   291	
   292	                // If the signal a) was previously clean or b) is an unowned derived, then mark it
   293	                if ((flags & (CLEAN | UNOWNED)) !== 0) {
   294	                        if ((flags & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   295	                                mark_reactions(/** @type {Derived} */ (reaction), MAYBE_DIRTY);
   296	                        } else {
   297	                                schedule_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (reaction));
   298	                        }
   299	                }
   300	        }
   301	}

    28	/*#__NO_SIDE_EFFECTS__*/
    29	export function derived(fn) {
    30	        var flags = DERIVED | DIRTY;
    31	        var parent_derived =
    32	                active_reaction !== null && (active_reaction.f & DERIVED) !== 0
    33	                        ? /** @type {Derived} */ (active_reaction)
    34	                        : null;
    35	
    36	        if (active_effect === null || (parent_derived !== null && (parent_derived.f & UNOWNED) !== 0)) {
    37	                flags |= UNOWNED;
    38	        } else {
    39	                // Since deriveds are evaluated lazily, any effects created inside them are
    40	                // created too late to ensure that the parent effect is added to the tree

    54	                v: /** @type {V} */ (null),
    55	                wv: 0,
    56	                parent: parent_derived ?? active_effect,
    57	                ac: null
    58	        };

    60	        if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag) {
    61	                signal.created = get_stack('CreatedAt');
    62	        }

    94	 * @param {Derived} derived

    97	export function destroy_derived_effects(derived) {
    98	        var effects = derived.effects;
    99	
   100	        if (effects !== null) {
   101	                derived.effects = null;
   102	
   103	                for (var i = 0; i < effects.length; i += 1) {
   104	                        destroy_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (effects[i]));
   105	                }
   106	        }

   114	let stack = [];
   115	
   116	/**
   117	 * @param {Derived} derived
   118	 * @returns {Effect | null}
   119	 */
   120	function get_derived_parent_effect(derived) {
   121	        var parent = derived.parent;
   122	        while (parent !== null) {
   123	                if ((parent.f & DERIVED) === 0) {
   124	                        return /** @type {Effect} */ (parent);
   125	                }
   126	                parent = parent.parent;
   127	        }
   128	        return null;
   129	}
   130	
   131	/**
   132	 * @template T
   133	 * @param {Derived} derived
   134	 * @returns {T}
   135	 */
   136	export function execute_derived(derived) {
   137	        var value;
   138	        var prev_active_effect = active_effect;
   139	
   140	        set_active_effect(get_derived_parent_effect(derived));
   141	
   142	        if (DEV) {
   143	                let prev_inspect_effects = inspect_effects;
   144	                set_inspect_effects(new Set());
   145	                try {
   146	                        if (stack.includes(derived)) {
   147	                                e.derived_references_self();
   148	                        }
   149	
   150	                        stack.push(derived);
   151	
   152	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   153	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   154	                } finally {
   155	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   156	                        set_inspect_effects(prev_inspect_effects);
   157	                        stack.pop();
   158	                }
   159	        } else {
   160	                try {
   161	                        destroy_derived_effects(derived);
   162	                        value = update_reaction(derived);
   163	                } finally {
   164	                        set_active_effect(prev_active_effect);
   165	                }
   166	        }
   167	
   168	        return value;
   169	}
   170	
   171	/**
   172	 * @param {Derived} derived
   173	 * @returns {void}
   174	 */
   175	export function update_derived(derived) {
   176	        var value = execute_derived(derived);
   177	
   178	        if (!derived.equals(value)) {
   179	                derived.v = value;
   180	                derived.wv = increment_write_version();
   181	        }
   182	
   183	        // don't mark derived clean if we're reading it inside a
   184	        // cleanup function, or it will cache a stale value
   185	        if (is_destroying_effect) return;
   186	
   187	        var status =
   188	                (skip_reaction || (derived.f & UNOWNED) !== 0) && derived.deps !== null ? MAYBE_DIRTY : CLEAN;
   189	
   190	        set_signal_status(derived, status);
   191	}
   192

   336	/**
   337	 * @param {string} path
   338	 * @param {string | symbol} prop
   339	 */
   340	function get_label(path, prop) {
   341	        if (typeof prop === 'symbol') return `${path}[Symbol(${prop.description ?? ''})]`;
   342	        if (regex_is_valid_identifier.test(prop)) return `${path}.${prop}`;
   343	        return /^\d+$/.test(prop) ? `${path}[${prop}]` : `${path}['${prop}']`;
   344	}
   345	
   346	/**
   347	 * @param {Source<number>} signal
   348	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
   349	 */
   350	function update_version(signal, d = 1) {
   351	        set(signal, signal.v + d);
   352	}
   353	
   354	/**
   355	 * @param {any} value
   356	 */
   357	export function get_proxied_value(value) {
   358	        try {
   359	                if (value !== null && typeof value === 'object' && STATE_SYMBOL in value) {
   360	                        return value[STATE_SYMBOL];
   361	                }
   362	        } catch {
   363	                // the above if check can throw an error if the value in question
   364	                // is the contentWindow of an iframe on another domain, in which
   365	                // case we want to just return the value (because it's definitely
   366	                // not a proxied value) so we don't break any JavaScript interacting
   367	                // with that iframe (such as various payment companies client side
   368	                // JavaScript libraries interacting with their iframes on the same
   369	                // domain)
   370	        }
   371	
   372	        return value;
   373	}
   374	
   375	/**
   376	 * @param {any} a
   377	 * @param {any} b
   378	 */
   379	export function is(a, b) {
   380	        return Object.is(get_proxied_value(a), get_proxied_value(b));
   381	}

    17		function throw_rune_error(rune) {
    18			if (!(rune in globalThis)) {
    19				// TODO if people start adjusting the "this can contain runes" config through v-p-s more, adjust this message

    21				let value; // let's hope noone modifies this global, but belts and braces

    47	/**
    48	 * Returns an [`AbortSignal`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/AbortSignal) that aborts when the current [derived](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$derived) or [effect](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect) re-runs or is destroyed.
    49	 *
    50	 * Must be called while a derived or effect is running.
    51	 *
    52	 * ```svelte
    53	 * <script>
    54	 * 	import { getAbortSignal } from 'svelte';
    55	 *
    56	 * 	let { id } = $props();
    57	 *
    58	 * 	async function getData(id) {
    59	 * 		const response = await fetch(`/items/${id}`, {
    60	 * 			signal: getAbortSignal()
    61	 * 		});
    62	 *
    63	 * 		return await response.json();
    64	 * 	}
    65	 *
    66	 * 	const data = $derived(await getData(id));
    67	 * </script>
    68	 * ```
    69	 */
    70	export function getAbortSignal() {
    71		if (active_reaction === null) {
    72			e.get_abort_signal_outside_reaction();
    73		}
    74	
    75		return (active_reaction.ac ??= new AbortController()).signal;
    76	}
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * `onMount`, like [`$effect`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect), schedules a function to run as soon as the component has been mounted to the DOM.
    80	 * Unlike `$effect`, the provided function only runs once.
    81	 *
    82	 * It must be called during the component's initialisation (but doesn't need to live _inside_ the component;
    83	 * it can be called from an external module). If a function is returned _synchronously_ from `onMount`,
    84	 * it will be called when the component is unmounted.
    85	 *
    86	 * `onMount` functions do not run during [server-side rendering](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/svelte-server#render).
    87	 *
    88	 * @template T
    89	 * @param {() => NotFunction<T> | Promise<NotFunction<T>> | (() => any)} fn
    90	 * @returns {void}
    91	 */
    92	export function onMount(fn) {
    93		if (component_context === null) {
    94			lifecycle_outside_component('onMount');
    95		}
    96	
    97		if (legacy_mode_flag && component_context.l !== null) {
    98			init_update_callbacks(component_context).m.push(fn);
    99		} else {
   100			user_effect(() => {
   101				const cleanup = untrack(fn);
   102				if (typeof cleanup === 'function') return /** @type {() => void} */ (cleanup);
   103			});
   104		}
   105	}
   106	
   107	/**
   108	 * Schedules a callback to run immediately before the component is unmounted.
   109	 *
   110	 * Out of `onMount`, `beforeUpdate`, `afterUpdate` and `onDestroy`, this is the
   111	 * only one that runs inside a server-side component.
   112	 *
   113	 * @param {() => any} fn
   114	 * @returns {void}
   115	 */
   116	export function onDestroy(fn) {
   117		if (component_context === null) {
   118			lifecycle_outside_component('onDestroy');
   119		}
   120	
   121		onMount(() => () => untrack(fn));
   122	}
   123	
   124	/**
   125	 * @template [T=any]
   126	 * @param {string} type
   127	 * @param {T} [detail]
   128	 * @param {any}params_0
   129	 * @returns {CustomEvent<T>}
   130	 */
   131	function create_custom_event(type, detail, { bubbles = false, cancelable = false } = {}) {
   132		return new CustomEvent(type, { detail, bubbles, cancelable });
   133	}
   134	
   135	/**
   136	 * Creates an event dispatcher that can be used to dispatch [component events](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/legacy-on#Component-events).
   137	 * Event dispatchers are functions that can take two arguments: `name` and `detail`.
   138	 *
   139	 * Component events created with `createEventDispatcher` create a
   140	 * [CustomEvent](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent).
   141	 * These events do not [bubble](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Learn/JavaScript/Building_blocks/Events#Event_bubbling_and_capture).
   142	 * The `detail` argument corresponds to the [CustomEvent.detail](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent/detail)
   143	 * property and can contain any type of data.
   144	 *
   145	 * The event dispatcher can be typed to narrow the allowed event names and the type of the `detail` argument:
   146	 * ```ts
   147	 * const dispatch = createEventDispatcher<{
   148	 *  loaded: null; // does not take a detail argument
   149	 *  change: string; // takes a detail argument of type string, which is required
   150	 *  optional: number | null; // takes an optional detail argument of type number
   151	 * }>();
   152	 * ```
   153	 *
   154	 * @deprecated Use callback props and/or the `$host()` rune instead — see [migration guide](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/v5-migration-guide#Event-changes-Component-events)
   155	 * @template {Record<string, any>} [EventMap = any]
   156	 * @returns {EventDispatcher<EventMap>}
   157	 */
   158	export function createEventDispatcher() {
   159		const active_component_context = component_context;
   160		if (active_component_context === null) {
   161			lifecycle_outside_component('createEventDispatcher');
   162		}
   163	
   164		return (type, detail, options) => {
   165			const events = /** @type {Record<string, Function | Function[]>} */ (
   166				active_component_context.s.$$events
   167			)?.[/** @type {any} */ (type)];
   168	
   169			if (events) {
   170				const callbacks = is_array(events) ? events.slice() : [events];
   171				// TODO are there situations where events could be dispatched
   172				// in a server (non-DOM) environment?
   173				const event = create_custom_event(/** @type {string} */ (type), detail, options);
   174				for (const fn of callbacks) {
   175					fn.call(active_component_context.x, event);
   176				}
   177				return !event.defaultPrevented;
   178			}
   179	
   180			return true;
   181		};
   182	}
   183	
   184	// TODO mark beforeUpdate and afterUpdate as deprecated in Svelte 6
   185	
   186	/**
   187	 * Schedules a callback to run immediately before the component is updated after any state change.
   188	 *
   189	 * The first time the callback runs will be before the initial `onMount`.
   190	 *
   191	 * In runes mode use `$effect.pre` instead.
   192	 *
   193	 * @deprecated Use [`$effect.pre`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect#$effect.pre) instead
   194	 * @param {() => void} fn
   195	 * @returns {void}
   196	 */
   197	export function beforeUpdate(fn) {
   198		if (component_context === null) {
   199			lifecycle_outside_component('beforeUpdate');
   200		}
   201	
   202		if (component_context.l === null) {
   203			e.lifecycle_legacy_only('beforeUpdate');
   204		}
   205	
   206		init_update_callbacks(component_context).b.push(fn);
   207	}
   208	
   209	/**
   210	 * Schedules a callback to run immediately after the component has been updated.
   211	 *
   212	 * The first time the callback runs will be after the initial `onMount`.
   213	 *
   214	 * In runes mode use `$effect` instead.
   215	 *
   216	 * @deprecated Use [`$effect`](https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$effect) instead
   217	 * @param {() => void} fn
   218	 * @returns {void}
   219	 */
   220	export function afterUpdate(fn) {
   221		if (component_context === null) {
   222			lifecycle_outside_component('afterUpdate');
   223		}
   224	
   225		if (component_context.l === null) {
   226			e.lifecycle_legacy_only('afterUpdate');
   227		}
   228	
   229		init_update_callbacks(component_context).a.push(fn);
   230	}
   231	
   232	/**
   233	 * Legacy-mode: Init callbacks object for onMount/beforeUpdate/afterUpdate
   234	 * @param {ComponentContext} context
   235	 */
   236	function init_update_callbacks(context) {
   237		var l = /** @type {ComponentContextLegacy} */ (context).l;
   238		return (l.u ??= { a: [], b: [], m: [] });
   239	}

   191	                }
   192	
   193	                source.wv = increment_write_version();
   194	
   195	                mark_reactions(source, DIRTY);
   196	
   197	                // It's possible that the current reaction might not have up-to-date dependencies
   198	                // whilst it's actively running. So in the case of ensuring it registers the reaction
   199	                // properly for itself, we need to ensure the current effect actually gets
   200	                // scheduled. i.e: `$effect(() => x++)`
   201	                if (
   202	                        is_runes() &&
   203	                        active_effect !== null &&
   204	                        (active_effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0 &&
   205	                        (active_effect.f & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0
   206	                ) {
   207	                        if (untracked_writes === null) {
   208	                                set_untracked_writes([source]);
   209	                        } else {
   210	                                untracked_writes.push(source);
   211	                        }
   212	                }
   213	
   214	                if (DEV && inspect_effects.size > 0) {
   215	                        const inspects = Array.from(inspect_effects);
   216	
   217	                        for (const effect of inspects) {
   218	                                // Mark clean inspect-effects as maybe dirty and then check their dirtiness
   219	                                // instead of just updating the effects - this way we avoid overfiring.
   220	                                if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
   221	                                        set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
   222	                                }
   223	                                if (check_dirtiness(effect)) {
   224	                                        update_effect(effect);
   225	                                }
   226	                        }
   227	
   228	                        inspect_effects.clear();
   229	                }
   230	        }
   231	
   232	        return value;
   233	}
   234	
   235	/**
   236	 * @template {number | bigint} T
   237	 * @param {Source<T>} source
   238	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
   239	 * @returns {T}
   240	 */
   241	export function update(source, d = 1) {
   242	        var value = get(source);
   243	        var result = d === 1 ? value++ : value--;
   244	
   245	        set(source, value);
   246	
   247	        // @ts-expect-error
   248	        return result;
   249	}
   250	
   251	/**
   252	 * @template {number | bigint} T
   253	 * @param {Source<T>} source
   254	 * @param {1 | -1} [d]
   255	 * @returns {T}
   256	 */
   257	export function update_pre(source, d = 1) {
   258	        var value = get(source);
   259	
   260	        // @ts-expect-error
   261	        return set(source, d === 1 ? ++value : --value);
   262	}
   263	
   264	/**
   265	 * @param {Value} signal
   266	 * @param {number} status should be DIRTY or MAYBE_DIRTY
   267	 * @returns {void}
   268	 */
   269	function mark_reactions(signal, status) {
   270	        var reactions = signal.reactions;
   271	        if (reactions === null) return;
   272	
   273	        var runes = is_runes();
   274	        var length = reactions.length;
   275	
   276	        for (var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
   277	                var reaction = reactions[i];
   278	                var flags = reaction.f;
   279	
   280	                // Skip any effects that are already dirty
   281	                if ((flags & DIRTY) !== 0) continue;
   282	
   283	                // In legacy mode, skip the current effect to prevent infinite loops
   284	                if (!runes && reaction === active_effect) continue;
   285	
   286	                // Inspect effects need to run immediately, so that the stack trace makes sense
   287	                if (DEV && (flags & INSPECT_EFFECT) !== 0) {
   288	                        inspect_effects.add(reaction);
   289	                        continue;
   290	                }
   291	
   292	                set_signal_status(reaction, status);
   293	
   294	                // If the signal a) was previously clean or b) is an unowned derived, then mark it
   295	                if ((flags & (CLEAN | UNOWNED)) !== 0) {
   296	                        if ((flags & DERIVED) !== 0) {
   297	                                mark_reactions(/** @type {Derived} */ (reaction), MAYBE_DIRTY);
   298	                        } else {
   299	                                schedule_effect(/** @type {Effect} */ (reaction));
   300	                        }
   301	                }
   302	        }
   303	}
   304

+                                        derived.f ^= UNOWNED;
+                                }
+                        }
+
+                        for (i = 0; i < length; i++) {
+                                dependency = dependencies[i];
+
+                                if (check_dirtiness(/** @type {Derived} */ (dependency))) {
+                                        update_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (dependency));
+                                }
+
+                                if (dependency.wv > reaction.wv) {
+                                        return true;
+                                }
+                        }
+                }
+
+                // Unowned signals should never be marked as clean unless they
+                // are used within an active_effect without skip_reaction
+                if (!is_unowned || (active_effect !== null && !skip_reaction)) {
+                        set_signal_status(reaction, CLEAN);
+                }
+        }
+
+        return false;
 }
